being officially labeled as a gang member by law enforcement agencies for wearing Juggalo related clothing or brandishing one or more Juggalo tattoos.&#8221;</p> <p class=\"p2\">Honestly, if this is true,&#160;they should march. This is America, and if you want to dress like some sort of twisted clown or claim that you work at a &#8220;dark carnival,&#8221; that&#8217;s you&#8217;re right. You shouldn&#8217;t lose your job for having bad taste.&#160;</p> <p class=\"p2\">Also, it&#8217;s some actual bullshit if Jared Leto helps <em>Suicide Squad </em>win an Oscar for essentially the same thing.</p> <p class=\"p2\">Go get &#8216;em, Juggalos.<br /><br /><iframe class=\"giphy-embed\" src=\"//giphy.com/embed/pKhKfSHVBUIJW\" width=\"480\" height=\"199\" frameborder=\"0\"
